Headers: MIME-Version: 1.0
Content-type: text/plain; charset=iso-8859-1
From: Techfest 2006<ayush@techfest.org>
Reply-To: ayush@techfest.org
Sub: Techfest '06
Mail: Hello there

Techfest, Asias largest science and technology festival, is back with its ninth edition, Techfest 06, to be held from the 20th  22nd January, 2006.

At Techfest 05 Drishti a competition to make aids for the visually impaired was launched. Taking off from where we left, Techfest 06 in association with the National Association for the Blind (NAB) and the Happy Hours Centre (HHC) presents Prayaas. Prayaas is an attempt to make the lives of the physically disabled simpler and more comfortable. Participants can choose problem statements from the website or one of their own and develop smart workable solutions. The teams must submit an abstract for the screening round outlining their solution. The solution may be supported by diagrams and graphs. Only the entries that make it through the elimination will be called to Techfest 06 to showcase their idea. 
Last date for registration and submission of abstracts is 20th December 2005.

For details vist http://www.techfest.org/smart_tech/prayaas/index.php

For querries contact:

Ayush Agrawal,
Manager, Smart Tech
Techfest '06
IIT Bombay
Ph: +91 98699-22308

Sub: Techfest '06
Mail: Hello there

Techfest, Asias largest science and technology festival, is back with its ninth edition, Techfest 06, to be held from the 20th  22nd January, 2006.

At Techfest 05 Drishti a competition to make aids for the visually impaired was launched. Taking off from where we left, Techfest 06 in association with the National Association for the Blind (NAB) and the Happy Hours Centre (HHC) presents Prayaas. Prayaas is an attempt to make the lives of the physically disabled simpler and more comfortable. Participants can choose problem statements from the website or one of their own and develop smart workable solutions. The teams must submit an abstract for the screening round outlining their solution. The solution may be supported by diagrams and graphs. Only the entries that make it through the elimination will be called to Techfest 06 to showcase their idea. 
Last date for registration and submission of abstracts is 20th December 2005.

For details vist http://www.techfest.org/smart_tech/prayaas/index.php

For querries contact:

Ayush Agrawal,
Manager, Smart Tech
Techfest '06
IIT Bombay

Mail: Hello there

Techfest, Asias largest science and technology festival, is back with its ninth edition, Techfest 06, to be held from the 20th  22nd January, 2006.

At Techfest 05 Drishti a competition to make aids for the visually impaired was launched. Taking off from where we left, Techfest 06 in association with the National Association for the Blind (NAB) and the Happy Hours Centre (HHC) presents Prayaas. Prayaas is an attempt to make the lives of the physically disabled simpler and more comfortable. Participants can choose problem statements from the website or one of their own and develop smart workable solutions. The teams must submit an abstract for the screening round outlining their solution. The solution may be supported by diagrams and graphs. Only the entries that make it through the elimination will be called to Techfest 06 to showcase their idea. 
Last date for registration and submission of abstracts is 20th December 2005.

For details vist http://www.techfest.org/smart_tech/prayaas/index.php

Sub: Results for The Simple Life v1.1 - Final shortlisting
Mail: Hi!

Following is the list of teams which have qualified for the next round of The Simple Life v1.1

SL06191 Outsourcing Online

SL06193 Industry-Villager Synergy

SL06195 Multiple Services Centre

--

Please note that the teams who have less than 4 people are open to expansion until Techfest '06. This means that if the team desires, someone visiting the website and wishing to contribute in their existing project can contact the team and join in. This will be done only with the consent of the team concerned and he/she should get the contact information through us. The contribution should be like any other team-member; developing a module, add-on etc. This does not mean in anyway that the teams who have less than four members necessarily need to expand.

A brief Synopsis of each project will be put up soon for people interested in applying to a project with less than four team members. In case of any doubts or discrepancies, drop a mail at avinavnigam@techfest.org

Also note that the final software will be judged on the basis of the abstract submitted and shortcomings would be penalised, if any.

In case of technical difficulties relating to the software development or the village, write to the email address mentioned and your query will be resolved as soon as possible.

Warm Regards,
Avinav Nigam
